NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
R. Durai a Male Child born to A. Raji, Hindu and born on 27th May 1981, residing at No. 39, 1st Street, Sri Devi
Karumariamman Nagar, Vijay Nagar, Velachery, Chennai-600 042, has been living as a Female after an elaborate Sexual
Reassignment Surgery on 29th April 2013, at SRM Specialty Hospital Ramapuram, Chennai-600 089, Surgery by
Dr. V. Jayaraman, (Regn:32070) Former Professor of Plastic Surgery, Kilpauk Medical College of Head of Upgraded Burns
Unit, Kilpauk Medical College Hospital, Chennai-600 010. By this I May be treated as a Female and henceforth
be known as R. SUJATHA.
R. DURAI.
Chennai, 2nd January 2015.

(Regn. No. 32070) Professor of Plastic Surgery, Head of Department of Burns, Plastic and Reconstructive Surgery, Kilpauk
Medical College Hospital, Chennai-10, By this I may be treated as Female and henceforth be known as Ms. G. RATHI.
G. RAJA.
